GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*(c6 - P/c7)*P + c8*P**c9

**Step 1: Simplify the GT expression.**

GT: `0.7214*(-1 + P/6.651)*(1 - P/13.538)*P + 0.7214*(1 - P/13.538)*P + 0.7214*P^(1/3)`

Let me expand the first two terms. Let me denote a = 0.7214, b = 6.651, d = 13.538.

First term: `a*(-1 + P/b)*(1 - P/d)*P`
= `a*(P/b - 1)*(1 - P/d)*P`
= `a*P*(P/b - 1)(1 - P/d)`
= `a*P*[P/b - P²/(bd) - 1 + P/d]`
= `a*[-P²/(bd) + P²/b + P²/d - P]`
Wait, let me redo:
= `a*P*[P/b - P²/(bd) - 1 + P/d]`
= `a*[P²/b - P³/(bd) - P + P²/d]`

Second term: `a*(1 - P/d)*P = a*P - a*P²/d`

Third term: `a*P^(1/3)`

Combining all:
- P³ coefficient: `-a/(bd)` 
- P² coefficient: `a/b + a/d - a/d = a/b`
- P coefficient: `-a + a = 0`
- P^(1/3) coefficient: `a`

So GT simplifies to: `-a/(bd) * P³ + a/b * P² + a * P^(1/3)`

Numerically:
- P³: `-0.7214/(6.651*13.538) = -0.7214/90.065 ≈ -0.008010`
- P²: `0.7214/6.651 ≈ 0.10846`
- P^(1/3): `0.7214`

**GT = c_A * P³ + c_B * P² + c_C * P^(1/3)** where these are specific constants, no dependence on t.

## GT Analysis

The GT is:
$$0.7214(-1 + P/6.651)(1 - P/13.538)P + 0.7214(1 - P/13.538)P + 0.7214 P^{1/3}$$

Let me simplify the first two terms. Let me denote $a = 0.7214$, $b = 6.651$, $c = 13.538$.

First term: $a(-1 + P/b)(1 - P/c)P$
Second term: $a(1 - P/c)P$

Combine first and second terms:
$a(1 - P/c)P[(-1 + P/b) + 1] = a(1 - P/c)P \cdot (P/b) = \frac{a}{b}P^2(1 - P/c)$

$= \frac{a}{b}P^2 - \frac{a}{bc}P^3$

So GT = $-\frac{a}{bc}P^3 + \frac{a}{b}P^2 + aP^{1/3}$

Computing constants:
- $\frac{a}{bc} = \frac{0.7214}{6.651 \times 13.538} = \frac{0.7214}{90.064} \approx 0.008010$
- $\frac{a}{b} = \frac{0.7214}{6.651} \approx 0.10846$

So GT ≈ $-0.00801 P^3 + 0.10846 P^2 + 0.7214 P^{1/3}$
